	y = 0

		}
	}

		base = 15
	}

	    popularity = 0.05
		}

	    popularity = 0.05
		}

    	target = KMV
    	modifier = took_stand_for_us
		}
	}
}

			}
		}

					size > 1
					include_locked = yes
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 2
				instant_build = yes
			}

		}

	cancelable = yes

	}

			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus CHI_Investing_Into_Heavy_Industry"

			limit = {
				arms_factory > 0
				free_building_slots = {
					building = arms_factory
					size > 1
					include_locked = yes
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			set_state_flag = CHI_Investing_Into_Heavy_Industry_mil
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				arms_factory > 0
				free_building_slots = {
					building = arms_factory
					size > 1
					include_locked = yes
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
